No. II(2)/HWMP/779/2018.вЂ”The Governor of Tamil Nadu 
having been satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule 
below are required for  Highways purpose to wit for the 
formation of over Bridge in between padalam вЂ“ Karunkuzhi 
Railway Station in lieu of existing Railway level crossing 
No. 64 and It having already been decided that the entire 
amount of Compensation to be awarded for the lands  to 
be paid out of the funds controlled and managed by the 
Divisional Engineer (Projects), Highways Department and 
after having considered by the cause shown by the owner 
or other persons having interest over the  lands, as the 
case may be, do hereby publish the following notice issued 
under sub -section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu 
Highways Act 2001 (TN Act 34/2002).
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the 
Tamil Nadu Highways Act 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 
2002) the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the 
lands specified in the schedule below and measuring 900 
square Meter of wet lands to the same or a little more or 
less are needed for the purpose of the formation of over 
Bridge in between Padalam вЂ“ Karunkuzhi Railway Station 
in lieu of existing Railway level crossing No. 64.  The plan 
of the lands under acquisition is kept in the office of the 
Special Tahsildar (Land Acquisition) inner Ring Road Scheme, 
Chromepet, Chennai вЂ“ 600 044 and may be inspected at 
any time during office hours. 
Schedule
Kancheepuram District, Maduranthagam Taluk, 
Karunkuzhi Village

as survey No.83/1 belonging to registered holder Thirumaal 
ayyar S/o.Raju ayyar bounded on the North by 83/1 part, 
south by 82A part, East by 29 part and West 82A part by 
vacant. вЂ“ 900 Sq.mt

HOUSING AND URBAN DEVELOPMENT 
Department
Declaration of intention to Specify the Area Comprising 
in Keeranur Selection Grade Town Panchayat to be a 
Keeranur Local Planning Area under the Tamil Nadu 
Town and Country Planning Act. 
[G.O.Ms.No. 114, Housing and Urban Development 
[UD4(2)] 9th August 2018, ГќВ® 
24, 
MГ·вЂ№H, 
FВјГµЕ“ГЂГµЛњ ГќвЂЎВґ-2049.]
No. II(2)/HOU/781/2018.вЂ”In exercise of the powers 
conferred by sub-section (4) of Section 10 of the Tamil Nadu 
Town and Country Planning Act, 1971 (Tamil Naud Act 35 
of 1972), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby declares the 
area comprising Keeranur Selection Grade Town Panchayat 
as a Local Planning Area and specifies the name of the 
said Local Planning Area as Keeranur Local Planning Area, 
the intention to do so having been previously published as 
required by clause (b) of sub-section (1) of Section 10 of 
the said Act.
S. KRISHNAN,
	
	
	
	
Principal Secretary to Government.
labour and employment Department
Notifications under the Employees' State Insurance Act. 
Exemption to the Tamil Nadu Fisheries Development 
Corporation Limited, Chennai for the period of one year 
from 19-07-2018 to 18-07-2019 under the Act
[G.O.(D).No. 430, Labour and Employment (L1), 16th July 
2018, ГќQ 32, MГ·вЂ№H, FВјГµЕ“ГЂГµЛњ ГќвЂЎВґ-2049.]
No. 
II(2)/LE/782/2018.вЂ”In 
exercise 
of 
the 
powers 
conferred by Section 87 read with Section 91A of the 
Employees' State Insurance Act, 1948 (Central Act XXXIV 
of 1948), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby exempts the 
Tamil Nadu Fisheries Development Corporation Limited, 
Chennai from the operation of the said Act for the period 
of one year from 19-07-2018 to 18-07-2019.
(1) The above exemption is subject to the following 
conditions, namely:-
	
(a) The aforesaid Management wherein the 
employees are employed shall maintain a Register Showing 
the names and designations of the exempted employees.
	
(b) Not withstanding the exemption, the employees 
shall continue to receive such benefits under the said Act 
to which they might have become entitled to on the basis 
of the contributions paid prior to the date from which 
exemption granted by this Notification operates.
	
(c) The contribution for the exempted period, if 
already paid shall not be refunded.
(2) The employer of the said management shall submit 
in respect of the period during which that Management 
was subject to the operation of the said Act (hereinafter 
referred to as "the said period") returns, in such form and 
containing such particulars as were due from it in respect 
of the said period under the Employees State Insurance 
(General) Regulations, 1950.
(3) Any Social Security Officer appointed by the 
Corporation under sub-section (1) of section 45 of the said 
Act, or other official authorised in this behalf shall, for the 
purpose of,-
(i) verifying the particulars contained in any return 
submitted under sub-section (1) of Section 44 of the said 
Act for said period; or
(ii) ascertaining whether registers and records were 
maintained as required by the Employees State Insurance 
(General) Regulations, 1950 for the said period; or
(iii)	 ascertaining whether the employees continue to 
be entitled to the benefits provided by the employer in 
cash and in kind, being benefits in consideration of which 
exemption is being granted under this Notification; or
(iv) ascertaining whether any of the provisions of 
the said Act had been complied with during the period 
when such provisions were in force in relation to the said 
workshops and stores be empowered to,-


844	
tamilвЂ‰ nadu вЂ‰governmentвЂ‰ gazette	
[PartвЂ‰вЂ‰IIвЂ”Sec.вЂ‰2
(a) require the principal or immediate employer to furnish 
to him such information as he may consider necessary; or
(b) enter any management, office or other premises 
occupied by such principal or immediate employer at any 
reasonable time and require any person found in charge 
thereof to produce to such Social Security Officer or other 
official and allow him to examine such documents, books 
and other documents relating to the employment of persons 
and payment of wages or to furnish to him such information 
as he may consider necessary; or
(c) examine the principal or immediate employer, his 
agent or servant, or any person found in such Management 
office or other premises, or any person when the said Social 
Security Officer or other official has reasonable cause to 
believe to have been an employee; or
(d) make copies of or take extracts from any register, 
account book or other document maintained in such 
Management office or other premises.
Exemption to the Tamil Nadu State Marketing Corporation 
Limited, Chennai for the period  of one year from 
01-10-2018 to 30-09-2019 under the Act
[G.O.(D)No. 479, Labour and Employment (L1),  
2nd August 2018, ГќВ® 17, MГ·вЂ№H, 
FВјГµЕ“ГЂГµЛњ ГќвЂЎВґ-2049.]
No. 
II(2)/LE/783/2018.вЂ”In 
exercise 
of 
the 
powers conferred by Section 87 read with Section 
91A 
of 
the 
Employees' 
State 
Insurance Act, 
1948 
(Central 
Act 
XXXIV 
of 
1948), 
the 
Governor 
of 
Tamil Nadu hereby exempts the M/s. Tamil Nadu State 
Marketing Corporation Limited, Chennai from the operation 
of the said Act for the period of one year from 01-10-2018 
to 30-09-2019.
(1) The above exemption is subject to the following 
conditions, namely:-
	
(a) The aforesaid Management wherein the 
employees are employed shall maintain a Register Showing 
the names and designations of the exempted employees.
	
(b) Not withstanding the exemption, the employees 
shall continue to receive such benefits under the said Act 
to which they might have become entitled to on the basis 
of the contributions paid prior to the date from which 
exemption granted by this Notification operates.
	
(c) The contribution for the exempted period, if 
already paid shall not be refunded.
(2) The employer of the said management shall submit 
in respect of the period during which that Management 
was subject to the operation of the said Act (hereinafter 
referred to as "the said period") returns, in such form and 
containing such particulars as were due from it in respect 
of the said period under the Employees State Insurance 
(General) Regulations, 1950.
(3) Any Social Security Officer appointed by the 
Corporation under sub-section (1) of Section 45 of the 
said Act, or other official authorised in this behalf shall, 
for the purpose of,-
(i) verifying the particulars contained in any return 
submitted under sub-section (1) of Section 44 of the said 
Act for said period; or
(ii) ascertaining whether registers and records were 
maintained as required by the Employees State Insurance 
(General) Regulations, 1950 for the said period; or
(iii)	 ascertaining whether the employees continue to 
be entitled to the benefits provided by the employer in 
cash and in kind, being benefits in consideration of which 
exemption is being granted under this Notification; or
(iv) ascertaining whether any of the provisions of 
the said Act had been complied with during the period 
when such provisions were in force in relation to the said 
workshops and stores be empowered to,-
(a) require the principal or immediate employer to furnish 
to him such information as he may consider necessary; or
(b) enter any management, office or other premises 
occupied by such principal or immediate employer at any 
reasonable time and reuire any person found in charge 
thereof to produce to such Social Security Officer or other 
official and allow him to examine such documents, books 
and other documents relating to the employment of persons 
and payment of wages or to furnish to him such information 
as he may consider necessary; or
(c) examine the principal or immediate employer, his 
agent or servant, or any person found in such Management 
office or other premises, or any person when the said Social 
Security Officer or other official has reasonable cause to 
believe to have been an employee; or
(d) make copies of or take extracts from any register, 
account book or other document maintained in such 
Management office or other premises.

ВЄГіvвЂ Г¬ВЈГівЂЎвЂ , В«ГЁВЈВ¬Гµ ГўВЎГё GЛњГµВЈГЁЛ†FЕёВ°вЂ№ В«ГЁВЈВ¬Гµ Г±ВЈГµвЂ Г¬

ГўВївЂ°В¶Е“Г·В¶ ГўВЎГЃ ГњГіВІ ГЁВјВ¶ГµГ®ВЈВЅвЂ№;
В«Г±ЕёВЄГЄВЈВЎГ№ Г®ГЁГіВЈPв„ў В«ГЁВЈKвЂљВ¬ГЁ ГўвЂЎ.1-Г¤ В«ГЁВЈВ¬Гµ 
ВЄГ®ВЈNГґВЈГ·Лњ cFГ±ВЎГёЛ†FВЎ bЛњЕ В№вЂљГЁВЈГЁ ГњГ‚Е В№ГµВ¶ ГњГµCГІВЄГ±ВЎГЃ 
Г®IвЂєГЇВЈВґ ГќГЂГЇЛњ ГњГµЛњГЁЕ“ ГЁВјВ¶ГµГ®ВЈВЅвЂ№;
1947-ГќвЂ№ ГќвЂЎВґ ВЄГ®ВЈNЕё Г®ГЁГіВЈГЃГЁЕ“ ГЄвЂ Г¬Л†FВЎ (Г±Л†FГІ

Г®IвЂєГЇВЈВґ ГќГЂГЇЛњ ГњГµЛњГЁЕ“ В«Г±ЕёВЄГЄВЈВЎГ№ Г®ГЁГіВЈPв„ў В«ГЁВЈKвЂљВ¬ГЁ 
ГўвЂЎ.1-Г¤ В«ГЁВЈГІвЂ№В№Л†Г‰Лњ ВЄГ®ВЈNГґВЈГ·Лњ cFГ±ВЎГёЛ†FВЎ bЛњЕ В№вЂљГЁВЈГЁ 
ГњГ‚Е Г°Е Г°Г¬ В«ГµвЂЎВґвЂ№ ГўВЎГЃ ГћГ®Г№ВЈв„ў ГќВ¬Г­JВґAГёВЈЛњ.

Г°ВЈв„ў Г ЕёГ°Л†FГІВЈЛњ ГѓвЂ ВґГёВѕ ГҐВЎPГІвЂ№ (ГµВ¬Гі) Г°вЂћГЄВЈГ°ВЈВ¬Г·ГІвЂ№, 
В«ГЁВЈВ¬Гµ ГўВЎГё GЛњГµВЈГЁЛ†FЕёВ°вЂ№ Г°ВЈГіbГІ В«ГЁВЈВ¬Гµ Г±ВЈГµвЂ Г¬ ВЄГ°ВЈВ¶ 
ВЄГ®ВЈNГґВЈГ·Лњ ГЄЖ’ГЁвЂ№ В«ГЁВЈВ¬Гµ ГўВЎГё ВЄГ®ВЈNЕёГЄЖ’ГЁЛ†FЕёВ°IВ¬Г¬В«ГІ 
ВЄГ®ВЈNЕёГ®ГЁГіВЈГЃ ГўВївЂ°В¶Е“Г·В¶ ГўВЎГЃ ГњГіВІ ГЁВјВ¶ГµГ®ВЈВЅвЂ№;

Г°Г¶Е Г°вЂЎВ¬Г­, ГЈЕёГЁВЈВґ ГўВЎГё GЛњГµВЈГЁЛ†FЕёВ°вЂ№ cГґГ±В¬ГґЛ† В«Г®ВЈвЂ Г¬Л† 
ВЄГ®ВЈNГґВЈГ·Лњ ГЄЖ’ГЁвЂ№, ГЈЕёГЁВЈВґ ГўВЎГё  ВЄГ®ВЈГ¶В¤ЕёГЄЖ’ГЁЛ†FЕёВ°IВ¬Г¬В«ГІ 
ВЄГ®ВЈNЕёГ®ГЁГіВЈГЃ ГўВївЂ°В¶Е“Г·В¶ ГўВЎГЃ ГњГіВІ ГЁВјВ¶ГµГ®ВЈВЅвЂ№;
В«Г±ЕёВЄГЄВЈВЎГ№ Г®ГЁГіВЈВ¬Гё В«ГЄГґвЂ№ ВЄГ®ВЈNГґВЈГ·Лњ cFГ±ВЎГёЛ†FВЎ 
bЛњЕ В№вЂљГЁВЈГЁ ГњГ‚Е В№ГµВ¶ ГњГµCГІВЄГ±ВЎГЃ Г®IвЂєГЇВЈВґ ГќГЂГЇЛњ

(Г±Л†FГІ ГЄвЂ Г¬вЂ№ XIV/1947) 10(1)(c) HKMВЅвЂ№, 10(1)(d) HKMВЎ 
ГµГівЂ№В№ GГ°вЂ°Г®В¬Г№JВЅвЂ№ ГµГ¶Ж’AВ»Е“Г· ГњFГЁВЈГіЖ’ГЁВ¬Г·вЂљ ВЄГЁВЈвЂЎВґ, 
Г®IвЂєГЇВЈВґ ГќГЂГЇЛњ ГњГµЛњГЁЕ“ В«Г±ЕёВЄГЄВЈВЎГ№ Г®ГЁГіВЈГЃ, В«ГЄГґвЂ№ 
ВЄГ®ВЈNГґВЈГ·Лњ cFГ±ВЎГёЛ†FВЎ bЛњЕ В№вЂљГЁВЈГЁ ГњГ‚Е Г°Е Г°Г¬ В«ГµвЂЎВґвЂ№ 
ГўВЎГЃ ГћГ®Г№ВЈв„ў ГќВ¬Г­JВґAГёВЈЛњ.
В«Г±ВЅвЂ№, 1947-ГќвЂ№ ГќвЂЎВґ ВЄГ®ВЈNЕёГ®ГЁГіВЈГЃГЁЕ“ ГЄвЂ Г¬Л†FВЎ 
10(2ГЈ) HKMВЎ WвЂє, ГћвЂ°Г® ГќВ¬Г­В¬ГІЕ  ВЄГ°ЕёГЃвЂљВЄГЁВЈвЂЎГ¬ 
ГЇВЈOLВјвЂ°В¶ ГЌВЎГЃ Г±ВЈГ®Ж’ГЁГЂвЂљВ°Е“ bЛњЕ В№ ГњOвЂљВ°Г±ВЈГЃ В«ГЄГґвЂ№ 
ВЄГ®ВЈNГґВЈГ·Лњ cFГ±ВЎГёвЂ№ В«ГЁвЂ ВґвЂљВЄГЁВЈЕ“Г·Е Г°ВґAГёВ¶.

ГўВїMГ№ВЈ
"ГЈЕёГЁВЈВґ, ГњГіВІ В«Г®ВЈвЂ Г¬вЂљГЁВ¬Гґ Г°вЂЎВ¬Г­Jв„ў FГ№вЂљГѓL 
ГњВ®Е Г°В¬Г¬Jв„ў 
WвЂєвЂљГЁВЈВµвЂ№ 
ГќГЃ 
ВЄГ®ВЈNГґВЈГ·ЛњГЁГЂвЂљВ° 
24-09-2015-вЂ№ В«Г®F, ГњВЎГЃ Г±вЂ ВґвЂ№ В«ГµВ¬Гґ ГµГ¶Ж’ГЁВЈГ±в„ў 
25-09-2015 ВєГ®в„ў eвЂЎВґвЂ№ Г°E ГњГ±ЛњЛ†FГІГ®ВЈв„ў ВЄГ®ВЈNГґВЈГ·ЛњГЁOВЎ 
ВЄГ®ВЈГ¬Лњ Г°E Г°ВЈFвЂљГЁЕ Г°ВґГµГ®ВЈв„ў ГњГµГіГµЛњ Г°EJв„ў В«ГЄЛњвЂ°Г® ГЇВЈЕ“ 
ВєГ®в„ў Г°EЛ†ВЄГ®ВЈГ¬ЛњвЂћCВ»Г¬ВЎ, HВЎГЄвЂ№Г°Г·вЂ№ Г±ЕёГЃвЂ№ ГЄвЂ Г¬Е Г°В®ГІВЈГ№ 
Г KВ¬Г±ГЁГЂвЂ№ ГµГ¶Ж’ГЁ В«ГµвЂЎВґвЂ№ ГўВЎГЃ В«ГЁВЈВјвЂ№ ВЄГ®ВЈNЕёГЄЖ’ГЁЛ†FВЎ 
В«ГЁВЈKвЂљВ¬ГЁ GГІВЈГІГ±ВЈГ№В¶Г®ВЈГ№ВЈ? 
ГќвЂ№ ГўQв„ў, Г KГІ Г Л†Г®ГіВѕГЁЕ“ HГёЕ HвЂљГЁВѕвЂ№.

ГЁВЈВјвЂЎГІВЈ Г°в„ўГЁВ¬ГґвЂљГЁГ¶ГЁвЂ№, (ГЁВЈВјвЂЎГІВЈ ГћВЎvВ®ГЋвЂ  ГќЕ  
ВЄГ¬вЂљГ№ВЈГґT ГњвЂЎВґ ГЄJВЎv) В«ГЁВЈВ¬Гµ Г±ЕёГЃвЂ№ ГЁВЈВјвЂЎГІВЈ 
В»QГµЛњCвЂ В® В®ГіvвЂ , В«ГЁВЈВ¬Гµ.
 
[ГњГіГЄВЈВ¬Г­вЂ‰(В®)вЂ‰ГўвЂЎвЂ‰484,вЂ‰вЂ‰ВЄГ®ВЈNГґВЈГ·ЛњвЂ‰вЂ‰Г±ЕёГЃвЂ№вЂ‰вЂ‰В«ГµВ¬ГґГµВЈЕ’Е В№вЂ‰вЂ‰(В®1)вЂ‰вЂ‰Л†

ГќвЂЎВґ-2049.]
No. II(2)/LE/792/2018.вЂ”ГћвЂ°Г® 
ГќВ¬Г­JВЎ 
ГћВ¬Г­Е Hв„ў 
В°PЕ HГ¬Е Г°вЂ ВґЕ“Г· ВЄГ°ВЈВјЕ“ ВЄГ®ВЈГ¬ЛњГ°ВЈГЁ ГЁВЈВјвЂЎГІВЈ Г°в„ўГЁВ¬ГґвЂљГЁГ¶ГЁвЂ№ 
(ГЁВЈВјвЂЎГІВЈ ГћВЎvВ®ГЋвЂ  ГќЕ  ВЄГ¬вЂљГ№ВЈГґT ГњвЂЎВґ ГЄJВЎv), 
В«ГЁВЈВ¬Гµ Г±ЕёГЃвЂ№ ГЁВЈВјвЂЎГІВЈ В»QГµЛњCвЂ В® В®ГіvвЂ , В«ГЁВЈВ¬Гµ 
ГќAГІ GЛњГµВЈГЁЖ’ГЁГЂвЂљВ°вЂ№ Г°ВЈГіbГІ В«Г°ВЈвЂљВ°ГµГіЛ†В¶ ВЄГ®ВЈNГґВЈГ·Лњ 
ГЄЖ’ГЁвЂ№, (H.ГўвЂ№.Гўv) В«ГЁВЈВ¬Гµ ГўВЎГё  ВЄГ®ВЈГ¶В¤ЕёГЄЖ’ГЁЛ†FЕёВ°IВ¬Г¬В«ГІ 
ВЄГ®ВЈNЕёГ®ГЁГіВЈГЃ ГўВївЂ°В¶Е“Г·В¶ ГўВЎГЃ ГњГіВІ ГЁВјВ¶ГµГ®ВЈВЅвЂ№;
В«Г±ЕёВЄГЄВЈВЎГ№ 
Г®ГЁГіВЈВ¬Гё 
В«ГЁВЈГІвЂ№В№Л†Г‰Лњ 
ВЄГ®ВЈNГґВЈГ·Лњ 
cFГ±ВЎГёЛ†FВЎ bЛњЕ В№вЂљГЁВЈГЁ ГњГ‚Е В№ГµВ¶ ГњГµCГІВЄГ±ВЎГЃ Г®IвЂєГЇВЈВґ 
ГќГЂГЇЛњ ГњГµЛњГЁЕ“ ГЁВјВ¶ГµГ®ВЈВЅвЂ№;
1947-ГќвЂ№ ГќвЂЎВґ ВЄГ®ВЈNЕёГ®ГЁГіВЈГЃГЁЕ“ ГЄвЂ Г¬Л†FВЎ (Г±Л†FГІ 
ГЄвЂ Г¬вЂ№ XIV/1947) 10(1)(c) HKMВЅвЂ№, 10(1)(d) HKMВЎ ГµГівЂ№В№ 
GГ°вЂ°Г®В¬Г№JВЅвЂ№ 
ГµГ¶Ж’AВ»Е“Г· 
ГњFГЁВЈГіЖ’ГЁВ¬Г·вЂљ 
ВЄГЁВЈвЂЎВґ, 
Г®IвЂєГЇВЈВґ ГќГЂГЇЛњ ГњГµЛњГЁЕ“ В«Г±ЕёВЄГЄВЈВЎГ№ Г®ГЁГіВЈГЃ, В«ГЁВЈГІвЂ№В№Л†Г‰Лњ 
ВЄГ®ВЈNГґВЈГ·Лњ cFГ±ВЎГёЛ†FВЎ bЛњЕ В№вЂљГЁВЈГЁ ГњГ‚Е Г°Е Г°Г¬ В«ГµвЂЎВґвЂ№ 
ГўВЎГЃ ГћГ®Г№ВЈв„ў ГќВ¬Г­JВґAГёВЈЛњ.

ВЄГ®ВЈNЕёГ®ГЁГіВЈГЃ ГўВївЂ°В¶Е“Г·В¶ ГўВЎГЃ ГњГіВІ ГЁВјВ¶ГµГ®ВЈВЅвЂ№;
В«Г±ЕёВЄГЄВЈВЎГ№ Г®ГЁГіВЈВ¬Гё ВЄГЄВЎВ¬Г№, ВЄГ®ВЈNГґВЈГ·Лњ cFГ±ВЎГёЛ†FГ№Вў 
bЛњMЕёГЁВЈГЁ ГњГ‚Е В№ГµВ¶ ГњГµCГІВЄГ±ВЎГЃ Г®IвЂєГЇВЈВґ ГќГЂГЇЛњ

ВЄГ®ВЈNГґВЈГ·Лњ cFГ±ВЎГёЛ†FВЎ bЛњMЕёГЁВЈГЁ ГњГ‚Е Г°Е Г°Г¬ В«ГµвЂЎВґвЂ№

27-01-2016 В«Г®FВ»вЂ№ Г±ЕёГЃвЂ№ FВј. M. ВЄГјГІГЄвЂ°FГіВЎ ГњГµЛњГЁЕ“ 
25-01-2016, 27-01-2016 Г±ЕёГЃвЂ№ 28-01-2016 ГќAГІ ГЇВЈвЂ ГЁOВЅвЂ№ 
Г°EвЂљВ° ГќГјГіВЈAВ»вЂ№ GЛњГµВЈГЁвЂ№ ГњГµЛњГЁГЂвЂљВ° Г°EГµГ¶Ж’ГЁMв„ўВ¬Гґ 
ГўВЎГЃвЂ№ В«Г±ВЅвЂ№ ГҐВ¶вЂљГЁЕ Г°вЂ Г¬ Г°EВ¬ГІ ВЄГЄЕ’ГІВЈГ±в„ў ГћВјвЂ°Г®Г®ВЈГЁ 
Г вЂЎВ¬Г±вЂљВ° В№ГёвЂ№Г°ВЈГ№ В°ЕёГёГЄВЈвЂ В®В¬Г№ ГѓP "No work No pay" 
ГўВЎГЃ ГњPMЛ†В¶ GЛњГµВЈГЁвЂ№ 28-01-2016 В«Г®FJвЂ Г¬ ГЁВ®Г®вЂ№ 
ГµВЈJГґВЈГЁ ГЎFГІвЂ№ ГµГ¶Ж’ГЁВЈГ±в„ў ГћВјЕ Г°В¶  ГЄвЂ Г¬MВ«ГіВЈГ®Г±ВЈГ№В¶ 
ГўВЎГЃ ГњPMЛ†В¶ В«Г±ЕёГЁвЂЎГ¬ ВЄГ®ВЈNГґВЈГ·ЛњГЁГЂвЂљВ° В«Г±В«Гґ В°PЕ HвЂ Г¬ 
В«Г®FвЂљВ° ГЎFГІвЂ№ ГµГ¶Ж’ГЁ В«ГЁВЈВјвЂ№ ВЄГ®ВЈNЕёГЄЖ’ГЁЛ†FВЎ В«ГЁВЈKвЂљВ¬ГЁ 
GГІВЈГІГ±ВЈГ№В¶ Г®ВЈГ№ВЈ? ГќвЂ№ ГўQв„ў Г KГІ Г Л†Г®ГіВѕГЁЕ“ HГёЕ HвЂљГЁ.
Г®IвЂєГЇВЈВґ ГњГіВІ В«Г°ВЈвЂљВ°ГµГіЛ†В¶вЂљ ГЁГ¶ГЁвЂ№,  
FВјВЄГЇв„ўВ«ГµL.

В«Г°ВЈвЂљВ°ГµГіЛ†В¶ ВЄГ®ВЈNГґВЈГ·Лњ ГЄЖ’ГЁвЂ№, (CГ¤В®В») FВјВЄГЇв„ўВ«ГµL ГўВЎГё

HOME DEPARTMENT
Appointment of certain Official as Chairman in State 
Transport Appellate Tribunal, Chennai under the 
Motor Vehicles Act.
[G.O. (D) No. 1014, Home (Transport-V), 30th August 2018, 
ГќГµE 14, MГ·вЂ№H, FВјГµЕ“ГЂГµЛњ ГќвЂЎВґ-2049.]
No.II(2)/HO/797/2018.вЂ”In 
exercise 
of 
the 
powers 
conferred by sub-section (2) of Section 89 of Motor Vehicles 
Act, 1988 (Central Act, 59 of 1988) the Governor of 
Tamil Nadu hereby appoints Selvi. R. Kamalavathi, District 
Judge (now under compulsory wait awaiting posting order) on 
transfer as Chairman in State Transport Appellate Tribunal, 
Chennai in the existing vacancy.
	
  niranjan mardi,
	              Additional Chief Secretary to Government.
